<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вышвыривать.html>вышвы́ривать</a> (31517)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышвырнуть.html>вы́швырнуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výšvyrnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышвыривать.html>вышвы́ривать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyšvýrivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышвырнуть.html>вы́швырнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to throw out, to fling out, to hurl out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chuck out</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вышвырнуть.html>вы́швырнуть</a> (15804)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:швырнуть.html>швырну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">švyrnútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышвырнуть.html>вы́швырнуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výšvyrnutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышвыривать.html>вышвы́ривать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to throw out, to fling out, to hurl out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chuck out</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шед<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ший</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:действительный.html>Действи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 4a.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>вы-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-шед-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ш</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ий</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вышибать.html>вышиба́ть</a> (20931)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышибить.html>вы́шибить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výšibitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-шиби́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-šibítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***вышивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вышивать.html>вышива́ть</a> (21291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the corresponding perfective verb <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́шить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výšitʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to embroider</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>to embroider
<ul><li><dl><dd><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a>. Никитенко, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:дневник.html>Дневни́к</a></i> 1827:<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:девушка.html>де́вушка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:вышивать.html>вышива́ет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> пя́льцах, <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друга́я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:держать.html>де́ржит</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руке́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:игла.html>иглу</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> плутовской <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбка.html>улы́бкой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поглядывать.html>погля́дывает</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vot dévuška <b>vyšivájet</b> na pjálʹcax, drugája déržit v ruké iglu i s plutovskoj ulýbkoj na vas pogljádyvajet</i></dd><dd>here a girl is <b>embroidering</b> in (an embroidery) hoop whilst the other is holding a needle and, with puckish smile, looking at you</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вышка.html>вы́шка</a> (6171)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выше.html>вы́ше</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышка.html>вы́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышка.html>вы́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышка.html>вы́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вышка.html>вы́шек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>tower</li>
<li>control tower</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> higher education (from <i><a href = vnd.unilang:высший.html>вы́сшее</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:образование.html>образова́ние</a></i>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> higher mathematics, advanced maths (from <i><a href = vnd.unilang:высший.html>вы́сшая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:математика.html>матема́тика</a></i>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> capital punishment, death penalty (from <i><a href = vnd.unilang:высший.html>вы́сшая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мера.html>ме́ра</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ния</a></i>, supreme measure of punishment)</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>шка</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 1-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 3*a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выявить.html>вы́явить</a> (6373)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>яви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выявить.html>вы́явить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výjavitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выявлять.html>выявля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reveal, to display</li>
<li>to discover, to uncover, to bring to light, to identify, to detect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устранять.html>устраня́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выявленный.html>вы́явленные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тки</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Núžno býstro ustranjátʹ <b>výjavlennyje</b> nedostátki.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">One needs to quickly eliminate identified shortcomings.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>вы́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вить.html>вить</a></b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выявлять.html>выявля́ть</a> (14124)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выявить.html>вы́явить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výjavitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выявлять.html>выявля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyjavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выявить.html>вы́явить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to reveal, to display</li>
<li>to discover, to uncover, to bring to light, to identify, to detect
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:устранять.html>устраня́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выявленный.html>вы́явленные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тки</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Núžno býstro ustranjátʹ <b>výjavlennyje</b> nedostátki.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">One needs to quickly eliminate identified shortcomings.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>.
